¶here begynneth kalendre newe legende englande ¶the prologe firste treatyce presēt boke taken newe legende sayntys englande irelande scotlande wale theym vnderstande laten tonge atte theyr pleasure may occupyed therwith therby ye apte lerne resydue shall hole legende vnderstande yt nat oonly sayntes borne theyse countreys sayde legende ī lytell treatyse also dyuerse blessyd sayntes borne beyonde see came theyse countreys englande irelande scotlā de wale doynge notable thynge honour god profyte people preche theym faythe oure lorde sette people good ordre haue lyued blessyd lyfe ī theyse countreys gyue people example good lyuynge also sayde legende present treatyse accompted countrey came seynt augustyne appostell englande blessyd seynt gregorye beynge pope sent fro rome seynt paulyn seynt laurence confessoure dyuerse company preche faythe oure lorde people realme beynge idolatroures clerely alyenatyd fro trueth wherupon seynt augustyne faythfully accomplysshynge auctoryte company conuertyd seynt ethelbert kynge kent people fayth lorde seynt paulyne conuerted seynt edwyn kynge northamhumbre people whiche countreys church buylded temple idollys destroyed turned church bysshoppes preestes ordeyned countrey fayth gladly resceyued great deuocyon ye deth seynt augustyne kyng ethelbert kynge edbalde yt sone kynge ethelbert fell idolatrye forsakynge cristen fayth wherby faythe lyke haue holly perysshed ye sayd seynt laurēce busshop caūterbury next seynt augustyne especyall myracle seynt peter reduced agayne faythe lyfe seynt laurence apperyth longe theyr tyme holy men seynt adryan seynt honorye seynt felyx seynt beryn dyuers cam fro beyonde see moche edefyed people ī realme englande establysshed greatly fayth whiche seynt augustyne seynt paulyne seynt laurence theyr company begon also dyuerse countreys englande whiche nat holly conuerted seynt augustynes dayes dayes fell agayne idolatrye thē reduced fayth lord neuerthelesse ryght fewe realme englande specyally ye cōmen people haue harde suche men soo moche yt ye oonly herynge theyr name wyll lernynge men wyll dyuerse blessyd men woman borne ī realme whiche haue done many notable thynges comen welthe people therof well ꝓfytable lyfe ye lyfe come seynt dunstane seynt deus dedit seynt wylfryde seynt oswalde seynt cedd seynt chadde bysshoppes seynt ethelbert seynt edwyn seynt edgare seynt oswalde kyngys seynt sexburgh seynt ermenylde quenes seynt wallen seynt gylbert seynt wulryke dyuerse holy men woman sayd legende also treatyse apperyth gloryouse sayntys wt borne countreys apꝑyth fayth lorde hath ben p̄ched receyued greatly prosperyd realme many oure auncestours neyghboures frendes mercye lorde ye ioyes heuyn praye v people also grace goodnes lord heyrys apparaū te kyngedome heuyn lawe god nat ben knowen ī theyse party aūcestours myght ꝑcase haue lyued erroures wherfore moche boūden loue theym honoure lykewyse v helpe dyd helpe v aūcestours frendys veryly nowe thyse dayes hygh charyte ꝑfyte loue almyghty god oure neyghboure yt theyse blessyd seyntes leest desyre therto loue iustyce zele ye comen welthe lyke desyre brynge ye people good lyfe hole truste sure faythe ī lord ī theyse blessyd men woman wolde renewe ye face worlde brynge newe lyghte amonge people dyd tyme ye sayd gloryous seyntys florysshed shyned ꝑfeccyon vertues euydently wyll appere theym wyll rede theyr legende trewe mekenes inuyncyble pacyence symple obedyence heuenly wysdome ꝑfyght charyte loue iustice mercye pyte cōpassyon vppon theyr neyghbourys ryches pouerte pouerte ryches lyke vertues gracyous gyftes god many nedye outwarde within forthe replenyssed goostlye swetnes comforte syght worlde theyr owne syght vyle abiecte syght almyghtye god seyntes precyous syngulerly elect wherfore people irelande haue seynt patryke blessyd lyfe conuerted moche people faythe great honour theyr necessyties call vnto hym helpe great deuocyon lykewyse scotlande people haue seynt nynian cōmenlye called seynt tronyon great honoure cause wale haue deuocyon seynt dauyd blessyd lyfe confermynge establysshynge ye people faythe prechynge good example realme englonde euer occasyon fewe people comparyson multytude haue deuocyon thyse blessyd seyntes haue laboured welthe people realme ī tyme paste haue theym honoure countreys haue seyntes lyke case yet knowe ryght well seyntys heuyn ī suche fauoure almyghty god ye theyre prayer herde suche persones pray maye dowte redye pray v worship theym call vnto theym prayer helpe god forbede v shulde thynke saye contrarye thynkynge mynde sayinge wyse sayntes aboue ī heuen bynethe therfore haue mynde vppon v helpe v pray v thynke saye thynke playnly saye seyntys haue charyte charyte ī erthe moche haue nowe heuen hadde great charyte open great labourys hadde saluacyon people realme prayed theym callyd vppon doo thenne shall great charyte haue nowe heuen let v beleue seynt paule sayth charitas nun quam excidit charyte persone hath doth contynewe therin whyle lyueth seasyth heuen neyther dimynysshed encreasyd made thyse sayntes theyr charyte heuen nowe thenne wherfore great charyte made redy pray people callyd vnto theym helpe prayer aforesayde shall theyr great charyte haue ī heuen make moche redy pray specyally suche doth worshyp call helpe vnto thē ouer theyr prayer harde byneth erthe sofer ye blessyd p̄sence god must theyr prayer herde aboue ī heuen haue god p̄sent face face therfore sythen sure fyrste yt redye pray yt wyll deuotly call vnto sure also secōde theyr prayer shalbe herde lette v deuoutly wt harte call vnto helpe pray v ye grace lorde shall prayer shall opteyne v yt desyre nother thynge yt shalbe ꝓphytable v ye people realme englond honour gloryous martyr seynt george theyr chief patrone defēder whose prayer speciall protecciō haue ben ī tyme past p̄seruyd agaynste theyr enemyes ye grace lorde ī tyme come shalbe yet neuerthelesse also honoure theyse gloryous seyntes yt haue laboured ī coūtrey ye helthe ye people aforesayde shall therby ryghthyghly please theyr patron seynt george shall sayntes suche haue honoured deuocion ī tyme past amonge ye blessyd seyntes heuen one wyll one loue one full charyte ye honoure honour one honoure one honoure thynge herein mystaken nat spoken cōuenyēt englysshe dewe ordre shulde ouer shortlye touched nat suffycyētly exp̄ssyd wherby maner ꝑsone myght offēded take occasion excepciō yt wyll please hym take ye best ment charytably refourme ye legende nede shalbe takynge ye pryncypall intēt treatyse kalendre shewe ye name ye seyntes theyr coūtrey lye shal apperyth ferre ye legende doth moost comēly ī place shewe also lytell thynge theyr vertues myracles ꝑte theyr storyes shortlye towched yt maye preparatyfe begynnynge reduce people realme ye rather haue sayde blessyd seyntes loue honoure thynge loued honoured knowē almoche late tyme syth sayde legende gatheryd gyther suche maner nowe euery thynge treatyse shortly touched lyke kalendre legende cōsyderynge also parte tho sayntes sayd legende kalender eyther borne realme abydynge therin theyse countreys irelande scotlande wale veray ryght owe subiecte obedyent realme englonde semyth lytyll treatyce maye conuenyentlye callyd kalender newe legende englonde ¶moreouer next ye sayde kalendre foloweth lyfe seynt byrget shortlye abrygged holy blessyd wydowe lyfe ryght expedyent euery maner persone loke vpon moost especiall lyue imatrymony estate wydowhod yt may se grace vertue blessyd woman lyued degre rather encouraged desyre haue lyke hym countrey ye well gaue poore men pryuely lefte coū trey sought many prouyncys coulde fynde sayde well cam septon shepherd tolde hym shulde fynde syluer well came thyder set staffe grounde therof moche prayer wrote boke foure euangelystys yt suche honoure yt people durste open people thought ther accorde fully made bytwixt enemyes apon yt boke came glastonbury farre fro then buyldyd chyrche vppon ryuer lyuyd heremytys lyfe felle syke wherfore sent abbot glastonbury desyred myght buryed monasterye went worlde fourth kalendas february yere lord ccccc xii grete lyght seen body lyeth glastonbury ¶de sancto gilberto confessore seynt gylbert borne sempyngham ī youth abiecte ī faders house yt seruauntys dysdeynyd sytte hym mete scole lytyll prophytyd wente fraunce toke degre mayster came ageyne englonde began ordre sempyngham men woman labouryd coulde helthe wllys coulde prophytyd worde dede exaumple father lykyd conuersacyon well presentyd hym chyrches sempyngham tyryngton tyme ther fell lyghte temptacyon bytwyxt hym hostys doughter nyght folowynge thought slepe put hāde ferre bosom coulde plucke oute agayne wherfore feryd greatly lefte place virgyn oon vii began relygyon vppō aboue necessary lyuynge gaue pore men made preest went rome ye pope engeny haue relygyon cisteux assygnyd haue rule monasteryes pope wolde assent therto ne yet cysteux pope orderyd yt shulde appoynt men therto hym selfe dyd iourney moche famylyer seynt malachye busshoppe irlande seynt bernarde bretherne appoyntyd ye ruell seynt augustyne susters rule seynt benedycte euyr myslykyd eyther rulys refourmyd sent rule rome cōfermyd made xiii monasteryes wherin deth aboute seuyn hundred bretherne fyue hundreth susters louyd placys lyke moche put lyke dylygence one dyd rydynge apparell symple companye honest absteynyd alwey fro flesshe grete sykenes lent aduenthe absteynyd fro fysshel hadde table dysshe callyd ye dysshe ihesu wherin put mete pore men refuse good dyner hevsyd redynge prayer medytacyon wyntre somerlyke many clothys electyd one dyscyples mayster hym obedyent toke habyt chanon man werynge sockys helyd gowte also fyre fledde fro house prayinge hurte yere lorde god thousande hundred foure score ix day nonas february full good werkys good exaumples went lorde buryed honorably monastery sempyngham foundyd ¶de sancto godrico seruo dei heremita fader moder seynt godryke dwellid norfolke towne callyd walpole pore worldlye substaunce ryche vertues deuoutly prayinge lord yt myght haue chylde apte seruyce sone callyd goderyke youthe marchaūte vsynge feyrrys markettys went seynt andrewys scotlande soo rome came marchauntys water went brytayne flaunders denmarke wan moche good xvi yerys expendyd suche busynes went twyse rome oon tyme went seynt gyle tyme toke moder hym whiche went barefote came whome laste tyme solde gaue poore men lyuyd caerlyle vnknowyn wher many folkys began worshype hym wherfore went wood lyuyd herbys frutys house founde olde heremyte eyther callyd name yet neuer herde taryed hym tyll heremyte dyed seynt cuthberte apperyd hym bad hym go ierusalem crucyfyed lord come agayne wood callyd fynkale lytyll fro duresme yt iourney toke sustenaunce drye barley breed water chaungyd clothynge wasshed theym ne chaungyd shone tyll came yt stonys grauell growyn foot greuouslye yt flesshe bonys myght scarcely hange gedyr fleme iordane chauugyd hym wyshe fro tyme shone retournyd ageyne fynkale ryuer made lytyll house dwelled vnknowen dyuerse yerys lyuyd wt leuys rotys began laboure get hym mete laboure dyggyd grownde sewe made gardeyne neuer lay bedde ye groū de vnder hym stone vnder hedde thyngys eschewed idelnes wolde eyther prayer medytacyon laboure wolde stonde ye water thoughe froste snowe sometyme moneth together nyghtys tyll mornynge teth chakyid ī heed wolde sey thys greuous ye fyre hell moche greuous coulde wynter wolde go barefote yt foot sumtyme cut greuously yt man myght put ī fynger chose ye pryor duresme mayster wolde speke wt man wtout lycēse hym iiii dayes weke sonday mōday tuesday fryday also festys aduēt fro septuagesyme ester kepte scylence began enhabyt yt place neuer went thryse dyuerse tymes great fowle deseasys byles fowle mater body wt intollerable payne yet wolde take medycyne fayde worthy suffer payne offencys wolde make oon rubbe sorys wt salte ben xi yerys wyldernes great swellynge toke hym ye face body yt coulde scarcelye knowen great inwarde peyne though wormys consumyd hym alweyes toke pacyēce tyme drewe nere callyd ye bretherne leyde hym vppon asshes put hym stamyn cowle lytell made monke duresme went lord ye xii kalendas iune ye yere lorde god mclxx many great myracles yt lord hath shewyd blessyd man great temptacyons yt ye goostlye enemye ofte apperyd hym haue deceyuyd hym som tyme lyke pylgryme sometyme lyke woman tyme moche terrybly lykenes dyuerse bestys howe wt sygne crosse euer vyctory lady dyuerse seyntys many tymys apperyd hym cōfortyd hym shortnesse omyttyd ¶de sancto grimbaldo abbate confessore alfrede kynge weste saxonyssente fraūce monke callyd grymbalde made hym abbot monastery yt newely made ī wynchester seynt grymbalde gaderyd great cōpany mō ky taught thē diligētly letter good maners gaue great almys deuoute ī prayer oftymys vsyd vygyllys full good ensaumples great age lefte worlde went euerlastynge rewarde heuyn viii ide iuly aboute yere oure lorde viiic foure score viii buryed monasterye wynchester chaunce callyd hyde hadde great honoure ¶de sancto gudwalo ep̄o confessore seynt gudwalle borne noble blood ye partyes brytayne youthe put lernynge came age made preest busshope abhorryd worldly thyngys euer came hym prosperously worlde turnyd honoure god last seynge bysshopryke maner cheyn bynde hym worlde lefte dyscrete man went monasterye dyocesse nyghe monastery great rocke lyke ile yt see went nyghe aboute seynt gudwale cōtentyd oon felawe made hym lytyll house stone lackyd water strake staffe rocke prayer feyre wellsprange therof gatheryd hundred foure score bretherne ye see nygh monasterye grownde verye lytell many ꝑsonys wherfore went see syde set staffe ye groūde chargyd see name lord ihesu crist yt shulde passe marke see obeyed vnto hym tyme sent discyples place great rayne fell cō trey merytes felle none ye wey discyples helyd wolfe yt hurte fote cō maūdyd hym shuld neuer doo hurte creature shulde euer ete hey lyke oxe dyd tyme pore man askyd hym almes bycause thynge hande gaue hym horse seruauntys morowe grudgyde came noder horse lyke ye horse ī euery thynge yet toke put werke seynt myghell arcaungell apperyd hym tolde hym veray daye shulde leue worlde anon gon seynt peter seynt paule apperyd hym cōfortyd hym dyed viii ide iune bodye leyde weyne caryed certeyne place haue ben buryed ox made vnmouable coulde goo styre wherfore cōmen assent two wylde kyne put weyne went streyght ile callyd plecyt honorably buryed many yerys fere enemy people ile fledde wey dyuerse countreys brederne seynge men flee toke body went fraūce cleremoū te blessyd relykys leyde lorde hath shewyd hym many myracles de sancto gundleo rege confessore seynt gundleus sone kynge southe brytons faders deth deuydyd realme seuyn ꝑtys gaue syx bretherne theyr porcyons obeyed hym theyr superyor sone callyd cadoke wyfe lay theyr bedde aūgell apperyd sayd lorde wolde yt shulde turne theyr hertys seruyce shewyd theym yt mornynge shuld goo lytyll hyll ryuer syde saw whyte oxe stāde shuld abyde ye mornynge ye kynge lefte realme seynt cadoke sone went ye sayd hyll ye aungell sayd foūde whyte oxe made churche lyuyd ī great abstynēce ete barley brede wherof thyrde parte asshes dranke water wolryse ye nyghtys bathe hym ī ye water wolde lyue ī owne laboure sone seynt cadoke thē beynge abbot nancarbanense came vysyte hym seynt cadoke sayd y• kyngedome heuyn promysyd yt begyn well theym yt ꝑseuer lacke water seynt gundleus prayed strake staffe grounde anon feyre well sprange vp tyme drewe nere sent seynt dubryce busshope landauēse sone cadoke comfortyd hym howselyd hym went lorde iiii kalendas apryll aungellys haue ben ofte seen visytynge ye place buryed dyuerse men haue ben greuously punysshed wronge doynge chyrche ¶de sancto guthlaco confessore seynt guthlake borne tyme ethelrede kynge marsh kynges blode byrthe hāde seen ye dore lyke hande redde man heuenly coloure makynge crosse vppon ye dore xxiiii yere age gaue hym selfe actys chyualry defē dyd hys father myghtely agaynste enemyes bette downe castellys towny moost cruelty also mercyfull wolde geue enemyes ye thyrde parte yt geet consyderyd yt glorye ye worlde smoke vapoure small abydynge wherfore caste away armoure went repē toke order geuynge hym monastycall lernynge wolde drynke nothynge yt myght occasyon dystemperaunce went crowlande man durste enhabyte fere wyckyd spiritis lyuyd blessyd lyfe sufferyd great temptacyons persecucyons wyckyd spiritis yt legende apperyth great length ofte delyuerd owte trowbles temptacyons seynt bartylmew synguler deuocyon tyme two deuyllys lykenes men came hym ꝑswadyd hym faste two thre dayes hole wekys put hym ī mynde moyses hely howe fastyd fastyngys olde father sythye thē knewe wyckyd spiritis wherfore made prayer anon vanysshed awey toke sustenaunce barley brede wonte blessyd man suche hoole entent god yt neuer harte pyte charyte mouth nothynge lorde ihesu pea mercy forgyuynge neuer seen angry prowde heuy alwayes īoon sobrenes tyme sawe two deuyllys wepe askyd ye cause wepte sayd bycause p̄uaylyd ofte agaynste thē made ye sygne ye crosse anon vanysshyd away ye busshope hedda goinge seynt guthlake praysid moch ye strayghtnes lyfe oon chapleyns sayd yt seen many heremytes good euyll one seen hym sayd coulde tell whether good ye fame rāne vppō hym whē cam seynt guthlake spyryt knowynge wordys askyd hym howe sayd yt man yt spake ye day abasshyd fell downe askynge hym forgyuenes thē ye busshope made hym preest suster callyd pega wolde see ī lyfe ye entēt myght ye rather mete lyfe come tyme drew nere shewyd discyple bertelyn therof bade hym yt shulde praye suster se hym buryed bertelyn prayed seynt guthlake shewe hym yt seen euery day syth fyrste cūmynge hym spekynge wt hym mornynge euenynge sayde yt euer syth came yt wyldernes aūgell cōforte hym helpe hym tēptacions shewyd hym thynges come wt great secretys yt laufull speke bade bertelyn kepe secrete shew ꝑsone suster pega holy anker callyd egbert thus spokyn came swete smell mouthe rose flowrys balme fro mydnyght mornynge great lyght seen ye house sayd dyscyple yt tyme come lyftynge vp ien hādys heuyn slepte ī lorde aboute ye yere grace viic vi aboute yere deth body remouyd foūde vncorrupt wt clothys kynge callyd ethelbalde wrongefully put realme moche famylyer seynt gutlake lyfe came tumbe prayed deuoutly hym helpe apperyd hym tolde hym yt within two yerys shuld restoryd kyngdō thē buylded crowlāde endewyd wt great lōdes many lybertyes hadde promysed seynt guthlake lyfe wolde doo de sanctum helena regina seynt helyn doughter cloell kyng grete brytayn ī tho dayes ye senate romesēte cōstā cyus subdued thē ye coūtrey spayne subdue also brytayne callyd englōde cloell ferynge ye great wysdome cōstancius anon assentyd pay y• olde trybute theruppon constancyus toke ye sayd helyn doughter wyfe constantyne whiche deth fader went rome great power brytayne toke moder wt hym put downe maxencyus ye tyraūte made emperoure cōuertyd ye feyth also crystenyd seynt syluester wherfore moder praysyd hym yt lefte ye worshyppynge idollys thought shuld rather haue receyuyd feyth ye god ye iues thē receyuyd receyue ye feythe man crucyfyed vppon tyme appoyntyd betwyxte haue bothe lawes disputyd day ꝓfounde argumētys seynt syluester also myracles yt lorde shewyd ꝓue feyth seynt helyn ye docturys ye iues yt brought wt cōuertyd ye feyth crystenyd encouragyd selfe enlarge ye crysten feythe yt could went iherusalem great power foū de ye holy crosse ye thre naylys crybbe yt lorde leyed ꝑte ye hey ladyes smokke made monasteryes lord sufferyd deth passyon ye holy crosse foūde bethelē many placys went ynde made many churchys brought ye bodyes thre kynges coleyne broughte ꝑte ye holy crosse constantynople went rome grewe suche hyghe charyte yt moder personys laye syke sawe heuyn open lord standynge great multytude aūgellys crosse meruaylously shynynge comfortyd moche went lord xv kalendas septēber honorably buryed ye pope wt great wepynge ye people sayd body trāslatyd constantynople lyeth venys de sancto henrico heremita seynt henry heremyte borne denmarke tyme thynge ordeynyd yt shuld haue ben maryed lord prohybytyd hym maryed bad hym kepe hym selfe clene inmaculate fro worlde shuld goo ile coket came tynmouth leue pryor go ile coket certen yerys lyuyd brede water ete thryfe ī weke thre dayes ye weke kept • cylence tyme wolde haue goon duresme yt hadde bote goo ouer water made prayer bote ferther syde brake yt tyed came ouer hym went ouer therin frendys herynge sent hym mouyd hym come agayne coūtrey seyinge dyuerse solytary placys yt countrey apte lyue solytary lyfe somwhat affeccyon ye coūtrey mouyd therto nyght folowynge made prayer ye crucyfyx knowe ye wyll lorde great deuocyon crucyfyxe spake vnto hym bad hym perseuer strongly yt begon yt shuld leue yt ile thende lyfe herynge laye prostrat besought lorde yt shuld haue power goo though wolde anon great swellynge felle knee grewe greuous yt sate agaynste ye sone wormys came oute wolde take vppe byd goo agayne yt theyr inherytaūce lyue yt norysshyd greuouse yt desease grewe ye gladde yeldynge euer thākyngys lord thoughe sykenes waxyd moche greuous yet wolde alone abydynge werynes ye longe nyghte without helpe whan ye houre deth came toke bell rope hande rynge ye bell deꝑtyd monke rynge ye bell rynge ranne thyder foūde hym deed syttynge vppon stone ye bell rope hande candell standynge hym lyghtyd heuenly lyghte body clēsyd fro ye fylthe anon whyte snowe nothynge apperynge fyrste desease face shone bryghtnes yt coulde scarsly knowen dyed ye yere lorde thousande hundred xx xvii kalendas february lyeth tynmouth farre fro body seynt oswyne ¶de sctīs hewaldo nigro hewaldo albo mtibus seynt wylly brorde felowes cōuertyd moch people fryselōde ye feyth two blessyd men borne englonde whiche callyd hewalde longe tyme ben irlonde went olde saxonye p̄che ye worde god dyuersyte theyr ye oon callyd ye blacke hewalde ye whyte hewalde came fryselonde harbored husbāde man desyred yt myght cōueyed ye ruler coūtrey message hym ꝓmysyd thē shuld taryed wt hym certeyn tyme ye harbarouse people herynge yt noder relygyon vsyd moche prayer dayly dyd sacryfyce sayde dayly masse suspectyd yt shuld speke wt theyr ruler shuld cōuerte hym ye crysten feyth ye ꝓuynce lyke folow leuynge theyr olde lawe wherfore kyllyd bothe v nonas october whyte hewalde shorte martyrdome blacke hewalde longe cruell tourmentys caste ye ryuer ryne ruler herde therof sore angry yt wolde let speke hym sendynge thyder kyllyd tho barbarous people yt kyllyd ye blessyd martyr also burnyd towne ye bodyes sayd blessyd men went xl myle ageyne streme place theyr felowys bryghte shynynge beame seen euery nyght bodyes lay takyn vppe buryed honorablye lyke gloryous martyr pipinus ye frenshe kynge remouyd theyr bodyes coleyne tho partyes theyr feest halowyd great deuocyon ¶de sanctum hilda virgine abbatissa seynt hylda doughter hereyce neuew kynge edwyn kynge edwyn cōuertyd prechynge seynt paulyn seynt hylda also cōuertyd anon lefte scler habyte decreed serue lord went ye kynge eest englond kyn desyrynge hym helpe yt myght go suster hereswida fraūce yt nōne ye monastery cale ben yere aboute ye purpose seynt • dan brought agayne owne countrey made abbesse monastery herthey whiche foūdyd blessyd woman callyd bega yt fyrste nōne yt euer ꝓuynce northamhūbre seynt hylda foū dyd monastery streneshalch callyd whytbye coūceyll holy men orderyd fyrst monastery reguler discyplyne orderyd monastery taught prety abstynence vertues especyall haue pea charyte great wisdome yt pore men also kyngys pryncys wolde aske coūceyll prayer great multytude serpentys yt feryd susters soo yt durste scarcely come theyr sellys turnyd stonys seruaūte cōmaūdement bad grete flocke gee yt destroyed corne monasterye go certeyn grounde yt enclosyd without taryenge went thyder hym bydden came thyder bade theym goo wolde oon byrdys yt deed reysyd lyfe bad goo felowys dyd wyll lorde great contynuell sykenesse vi yerys dyed vii yere great inwarde peyne lefte worlde ye xv kalendas december nonne monastery callyd hacanos seynt hylda lytyll deth foundyd xiii myle fro then seynt hylda sawe sowle borne heuyn great company aungellys ¶de sanctum hildelitha virgine abbatissa seynt hyldelythe abbesse barkyng next seynt alburgh lyuyd vnto great age ī kepynge reguler obseruaūcys exortacyons good cōuersacyon couragyd men heuenly thynges next seynt alburgh feest solempnysed barkynge great honoure seynt hyldelythe oonly honour seynt dūstane seynt ethelwolde seynt elphege also many olde holy faders holynesse cōmendyd wryttyn yt full charyte techer vertue gyuer good exaūples vygyllys fastyngys benygnyte mercye wt great dylygens ꝓuydyd yt nedyd bothe body sowle god man lyuyd without offēce apperyth lyfe myracles ye thre blynde woman came oon tyme oon seynt alburgh noder seynt hyldelythe thyrde seynt wulfhylde receyuyd thre theyr syghte ¶de sancto honorio archiep̄o confessore seynt honorye discyple seynt gregory seynt iustus electyd archebusshope caūterbury cōsecrate paulyn archebusshope yorke pope honoryus sent hym pall wt letter wherin decreyd yt whether archebusshope caūterbury yorke dyed furste yt y• ouerlyuyd shulde haue auctoryte make newe goo euery tyme rome great iourneys blessyd man made seynt felyx busshope eest englonde conuertyd coūtrey feythe seynt edwyn deed coūtrey northamhūbre trowblyd paganes seynt paulyn quene ethelburghe wyfe kynge edwyn went seynt honorye made seynt paulyn busshope rochester quene ethelburghe nonne place callyd lymmynge foundyd monasterye vppon groūde yt gyfte broder kynge edbalde mother many virgyns wydowys blessyd man made parysshys ordeynyd clerkys p̄chourys bad shulde instructe people aswell feyrenes pacyence hygh doctryne yt rude people myght broughte loue almyghty god aswell swete techynge sharpenes drede lord adournyd blessyd man pure feythe goodlye conuersacyon many sygnys vertues yt shone realme englonde lanterne put away errours cō uertyd many paganes feythe releuynge wretchydnes people prayer consolacyon lyfe shone lyke glasse yt wolde loke strayght harde hymselfe lyberall ye pore people seruynge lord ī humylyte charyte went ye prysone worlde ye day kalendas october yere lorde god syx hundred fyghtye thre lyeth monasterye seynt peter lyncolne stale cristen chylde aboute age viii yerys callyd hugh put hym ī secrete house fedde hym x dayes mylke yt myght abyde ye gretter turmētys thereupō sent ye towny englō de wherein iewys haue thē ye sacryfyce chylde entendyd crucyfye despyte lorde ihesu cryste gaderyd appoyntyd iuge pylat iugyd hym deth bet hym soo blode folowyd crownyd hym thorne spyt vppon hym mockyd hym euery man pryckyd hym knyfe gaue hym drynke gall great opprobryes blasphemouse wordys gnasshynge theyr teth callyd hym ihesus cursyd prophet crucyfyed hym spere thruste hym herte deed toke body fro crosse vnbowelde hym theyr enchauntementys leyde bodye grounde groūde wolde kepe caste vppe agayne wherfore merueylously aferde threwe hym pytte ye moder chylde made great sorowe dylygentlye enqueryd hym harde say seen laste iewys house pleyinge iewys chyldren went sodeynly house founde chylde vppon suspeccyon man owyd house takyn confessyd murder wherupon xviii rychest iewys lyncolne yt assentyd ye martyrdome ye sayd blessyd chylde drawyn hangyd chanōs lyncoln̄ askyd body ye sayde chylde buryed hym lyke gloryouse martyr ¶de sancto hugone ep̄o confessore seynt hugh whē viii yere olde set reguler discyplyne euer broughte vp vtue neuer knewe pleasurys ye worlde lernyd maner disportꝭ made chanon regler monastery grāmiople fader lyued vnder reguler discipline lōge fader lyued wiped shone made bedde dylygent hym thyngꝭ zele streyghter religion entred relygiō ye ordre chartuc made prest whan masse ordred hymself lorde ben visibly present vsed moch vigylles fastyngꝭ scorgynges ofte fasted brede water weer heere vse relygion made proctour thought slepe made hym prest came hym opened bely raser cut fro hym thyng lyke bylle fyre neuer felt temptacion flesshe myght lyghtly despyse desyre kynge henry seconde sent englande pryor wythm̄ thoughe moche refused tyme whan came kynge certeyne thynges neded kynge gaue hym lytell comforte fayre wordes one gerarde came seynt hugh • sayd kynge wolde go home agayne countre tolde kyng sawe well al gaue soule helth thought loste seynt hughe bad hym leue suche wordes holde peace spake kynge suche sobre charytable maner yt doon kynge enbraced hym sayd verayly shuld neuer go hym yt wolde kepe hym take counsell hym helth soule anone gaue seynt hughe asked one tyme kynge great ꝑell see great truste ye prayer seynt hughe bretherne sayd aduowed came safe lande wolde make hym bysshop forthwith tempest ceasyd buyldynge done wytham wolde euer occupyed prayer redynge medytacyon spirituell collacion exortacion wolde neuer lye bedde wakynge eyther ryse go prayer īmediatly slepe agayne ye bysshop lyncoln̄ translated rome seynt hughe elected therto sayd wolde wyse take vpon hym wtout assent hedde house opteyned wolde nat yet agre tyll aserteyned hole assent chanons lyncoln̄ dean lyncoln̄ chyef chapiter came hym wytham herde hym speke desyred hym great ī staunce deuocōn take vpon hym assented ye firste nyght came bysshopryche harde voyce say hym slepe egressus e īsalutē ppli tui salutem cū xp̄o tuo seynt hughe accursed ye kynges chyef forster doynge agaynst lyberte ye churche wherfore ye kynge toke great displesure mater nat yet determyned kynge desyred hym one clerkꝭ noīacion benefyce voyde gyft seynt hughe denyed wherfore kynge angry sent hym came founde kynge syttynge amonge lordes kynge wolde nat water gleni whiche kyngdome bernyshe tyme fontes baptised also many ye water swala kyngdome deyre also prouynce lyndesey lyncoln̄ water trent six yeres whiche dayes kyng edwyn contynued prechynge baptisynge people kyng edwyn made hym bysshoppes see yorke began buylde hym churche stone ī honour seynt peter byfore fynysshed martyred seynt oswalde succeded hym buylded resede wetherof made dyuerse church one lyncoln̄ longe decayed yerely done myracles iustus yt bysshop deed seīt paulyn̄ made honorius bysshop longe stature somwhat stowpynge blacke heere lene faced venerable also terryble coūtenaūce ye good kyng edwyn martyred seynt paulyn̄ left iame deakon yorke came īto kent wt quene ethelburgh yt wyfe kyng edwyn brought wt hym goodly crosse chaleys golde yt yet shewe kent made bysshop rochester honorius ye said iames lyued tyme venerable bede ye yere lorde vic xliiii vi ide october chaūged lyf lyeth rochester left palle woman yt longe cōtynued synne tyme goynge offer hym stopped ye first gresse dyuers tymes sawe nothyng wherby moche cōpuncte prayed ye monkꝭ pray cōfessyd yet neuerthelesse fel agayne wher syke meruaylously sore aferde harde iugemēt god confessed ye bysshop sent offrynge seynt paulyn̄ seyinge seynt paulyne receyue myne offryng forgyuen nat shal haue euer lastynge payne sent thyder receyued firste refused regarded nat offrynge • entaunce woman ¶de sancto petroco abbate confessore seynt petroke borne cumber kynges sone fro youth folower ye appostellys sober meke feruent charite redy merkes relygyon shuld haue ben made kynge forsoke pompe world toke hym lx felowes entered relygyon went irlande xx yeres profited moche lernynge entendynge go agayne coū tre founde shyp redy left without keper whan came brytayne founde men labouryng spake harde wordes hym whether tempte holynes restreyne theyr drynesse bad hym make welle swete water rocke therby dyd harde holy man called sā pson yt ledde therby solytary lyf great streyghtnes wt barley brede ī fastyngꝭ prayer sawe sampson prayed lorde yt shuld nat remoue tyll spoken wt hym prayer herde sāpson therby boūden tyll saluted eche nygh sāpson made monastery lyued theyr xxx yerꝭ ī great fastīgꝭ prayer colde restreynyng glotony vnlaufully mocyons tyme lyued suche innocencye yt dyd nothynge yt wolde nat haue done hym xxx yerꝭ went rome came agayne cornewayle wherin great tempest cōforte discyples sayd tempest shuld cease ye next day whan dyd nat heuy aud repented hym self moche p̄sūpcion yt sayd otherwyse folowed wherfore thirde day went rome agayne ier • toke purpose go ynde come wt great labour est occean foūde vessell mete oonly one man wherby went ilande lyued cō templacion vii yeres al tyme fedde one fysshe afterwarde aungell conueyed vessell west parte brytayne afore tyme ben cruell kynge gathered many venemous serpentes punysshe felon men offended deed sone wolde none y• crueltye one serpentes hunger kylled nother tyl one terryble serpent preuayled kylled man beste seynt petroke droue wyldernes shuld hurte man prayer byfore people reysed man fro deth lyfe shuld dye called disciple instructed theym shuld kepe ꝑfyght relygyon aduysynge theym ye forsaken wordly busynes shuld also eschewe desceytfull plusures world shuld thurst downe angre hatered fle fr • lye abanysshe enuye p̄pare hertes temple holy ghost full good werkes blessyd myracles chaunged lyfe day nonas iune ¶de sancto pirano ep̄o confessore seynt pyran borne irlande youth went ile called clera lyued great abstynense holy werkes xxx yeres went rome made bysshop seynt patryke bad hym go byfore hym irlande preche people shuld buylde monastery ryuer waram shuld cymbale soūde without touchynge done prechynge ye fayth encreasyd moche irlande exaumple many styred loue god forsakynge wordly thynges folowed oure lorde amonge brendane whiche made hym place nat ferre fro seynt pyran childe instygacion deuyll put fyre vnder lycour make drynke monkes wherupon seynt pyran sayd shalbe fyre place tyll lorde send fro aboue next daye ye childe kylled woode wolfe geran mayster childe came seynt pyran made prayer forth fyre fell bosom whiche dyd bere without hurtynge clothes shuld go souper geran sayd wolde nat ete tyll childe came lyue hym praye seynt pyran childe rose fro deth ete theym kynge toke fro moder seynt pyran kynges doughter called brunet brynge vp kept castell bond woman seynt pyrane spake hym sayd wolde nat delyuere • onlesse byttour mornyng waked hym slepe whiche thought ben vnpossyble ye nyght fell great snowe aboute castell seynt pyrane company fell none mornynge byttoure came castell noyse made wakyd kynge kynge lay prostrate fete seynt pyrane cryeng hym mercye delyue red damosell vnto hym neuerthelesse reputed delyuered wolde haue taken agayne founde deed wherfore moche angre sayd wolde put seynt pyrane fro place sayd hym nat god place nat almyghty godes kynge beynge veray angry gone fro hym sawe castell fyre quene hauynge ii sone lefte sone loued beste byhynde hast cōmytted seynt pyrane castell burned childe sauffe kynge greatly marueylyng came seynt pyrane sayd wolde gladly whatsoeuer bad hym offered hym two sone serue god kynge gone reysed brunet agayne fro de • h lyfe lord shewyd hym many myracles uys yt lyke haue ben taken cōmytted seynt pyrane sodeynly fyre rose woode bytwixt theuys theym wolde haue taken theym yt saued theym selfe came seynt pyrane taryed hym lyfe reysed dyuerse fro deth lyfe drowned also otherwyse deed went vpon ye water ceased fyre blessynge multyplyed meete fedde moche people tourned water wyne two kynges monycyon wolde nat cease fro batayle wherfore prayer great wodde bytwixt theym sodeynly felle downe stopped coulde nat mete togyther lyfe neuer ware bestes skynnes fro flesshe flesshely desyres absteyned strongely fro myght dystemper hym toke lytell slepe oft visyted aungellꝭ made many prestes clerkes cc yere olde dyed hauyng lytell sykenes neyther loste toth ne yet appeyred syght made enemy frendes dyd good euyll hadde mercye pyte vpon neyghboures moch laboured owne handes yt myght gyue wanne almes punysshed body fastynges vigylles colde hungre thurste dylygently kepynge charite chastyte hospitalite alway fro youth prayeng redynge techynge doynge good werkes humble gentyl speche wyse sobre mercyfull omytted nothynge cōmaū dementes god fedde hungry gaue drynke thursty receyued harborowles clothed naked taught bretherne loue togyther direct yt iye theyr mynde almyghty god alway desyre kyngdome heuyn called disciple tolde theym wyl god shuld go cornewayle shewyd many great trouble shuld come countre prayed theym praye hym deth myght fynde lorde meke plesaunte vnto hym came cornewayle made house lorde shewyd hym many myracles knewe shuld deꝑte transitory lyfe called disciple prechyd theym many thynges kyngdom heuyn caused graue made goynge deꝑted great bryghtnes thyrde nonas marche lyeth iu cornewayle nygh seuerne fro petrokstowe xv myle fro monshole xx myle ¶de sancto richardo ep̄e confessore seynt richarde borne ī diocise wigorn̄ wyche youthe eschewyd daunsynges vayne playes forsoke twyse maryed went stodye oxforde bonanye aurelian profyted moche lawe cannon dyuynyte made chaunceler seynt edmunde archbysshop caunterbury hym veray constaunte trouble lyberte church offyce refusyd take ony maner rewardys dyd iustyce ryche pore regardynge personys grete man small chosen busshope chichestre kynge henry thyrde wolde ī wyse assent eleccyon kept hym fro landys goodes went rome consecrate pope innocent ye fourthe retournyd towardys englonde cōmynge home vysytyd relykys mayster seynt edmōde came englonde suffred many great rebukys iniuryes great pacyence longe tyme tyll great sute restoryd possessyons blessyd man made busshope went aboute dyoces prechynge visytynge mynystrynge sacramentys fro then feruent prayer lyberall almes gyuynge dylygent aboute poore men demeanoure ye meke made place yt preestys felle pouerte myghte releuyd great man accursyd wronge doon churche came hym receyuyd hym famylyerly bade hym dyner sayinge tyme wolde assoyle hym tyme sentence shulde reuyue onlesse made amendys offendyd agaynste churche sayinge also partyes varye thynge clayme ryght yet ought shewe charyte eche man clayme yt maye yet withdrawe fro god whiche charyte sought poore men went vysytacyon wolde aswell owne presence almes comforte herd confessyons assoylyd penytentys gaue counceyll axyd strengthed men feruent serue god multyplyed brede yt fedde moche people reysyd chylde yt deed borne blessyd man prechynge pope auctoryte helpe holy lande dyed douer thyrde nonas apryll brought frothens chychestre lord hath shewyd hym many myracles ¶de seruo dei roberto abbate venerabili seynt robert borne prouynce yorke toke order preesthod benefice forsoke enteryd relygyon whytby lycence abbot went fontes rycharde pryor seynt mary yorke buyldyd monasterye man lyuyd idle gaue hym laboure bretherne went hungry theyr table wery bedde lyuyd without murmure heuynes great feruoure laudyd lorde seynt robert made newe monasterye made abbot neuer rose fro table fullysacyate fasted euery lent breed water estre tyme appetyte ete sayde thought eten brede butter shulde ete whan brought consyderynge somwhat assentyd concupyscence wolde ete sent gate poore men aungell lyke yonge man wt bryght shynynge face toke ye dysshe anon vanysshyd awaye dysshe askyd fell sodeynly vppon borde seynt robert sayde dayly besyde dutye c l psalmes went newe castell sawe deuyll amonge moche yonge people compulcyon shewyd seynt robert ne ben cōmynge made husbonde pompyouse bryde haue ben slayne enemyes vpon shulde haue folowyd great murdre cō mynge sayd purpose stoppyd nyght thought sawe dedyll amonge bretherne toke nouyce stable pullyd hym basket hoke mornynge seynt robert enquyred hym ren weye accōpanyed hym theuys shortlye heed stryken ghostlye fader seynt godryke dyed seynt godrykesawe thre aungellys bere soule heuen seynt godryke sayd purueyaunce god blessyd woman hastynges wente hym oonsorte oon rewarde heuyn dyed yere lorde thousande hundred lix vii ide iune whome oure lorde hath shewyd many great myracles dome man hadde lōge ben seynt thomas helpe bydden seynt thomas shulde goo newe monesterye seynt robert shulde helyd soo knyght sawe vysyon many deuyllys goo towarde ye newe monastery thought monke whyght apparell came monastery crosyer lyfte vppe prohybytyd yt shuld goo ferther thought theyr stryuynge crosse nygh hym throwne downe asapperyd sent thyder mornynge de sancto rumwaldo moder seynt rūwalde doughter kynge pēda paynym crystened maryed ye kynge northā humbre paynym prayed hartelye lorde body shulde neuer defoulyd man eschaungyd fro lawe came ye chaumbre tolde husbonde wolde neuer accūpany hym tyll crystenyd ye wyll lorde assentyd aftre quene great chylde goynge fader delyueryd tētys medowe besyde buckyngham callyd suttun anon chylde borne cryed cristen man thryse sayd wolde haue godfaders ryche prowde men ye worlde chase godfaders two holy prestis wyderynus edwoldus shewyd holowe stone shulde crystenyd moch people coulde remoue stone bade wyderinus edwoldus name lord brynge anon brought without dyffyculte crystenyd callyd rumwalde appoyntyd anon prechyd people hyghe mysteryes trynyte howe thre personys one god artycles feythe x commaundemē tys specyally loue almyghty god neyghbour exortyd people penaūce theyr synnys leue theyr euyll lyfe make amendys yt haue offendyd fastynges prayer almesdedys aduertysyd people loue honour eche accuse detracte stele ne forsworne made long sermon approuyd grete auctorytes scripture sayd hym lyue worlde aftre thre dayes spiryt went heuen ye thyrde nonas nouembre appoyntyd bodye lay oon yere borne two yerys brakley buckyngham lyeth day theyse towny tyme namyd callyd accordynge namyd lorde hath shewyd hym many myracles ¶de sancto sampsone ep̄o confessore seynt sampsone borne great brytayne lord shewyd vysyon moder callyd anne whiche bareyne lyuyd husbōde blessyd lyfe fastyngys prayer shuld haue sone shuld call sāpson yt shulde great lorde worthye haue order preesthod vii yerys olde commyttyd seynt iltut sayde shuld great busshope profyte moche chyrche god toke dekon preesthod also made busshope whyte doue seen descende vppon hym hyer degre yt toke ye streyghter lyfe ledde ī lyfe neuer ete flesshe celerer neuew seynt iltute desyrous abbot aftre vncle feryd yt seynt sāpsone shuld haue wherfore put great poyson chales blessyd dranke without hurte celerer abydynge malyce shulde houselyd seynt sapsone sonday deuyll enteryd hym vexyd hym sore seynt sampsone delyueryd water oyle blessyd gaue hym daye labouryd prayed nyghte redde scripture vsyd medytacyon toke slepe lenyd wall neuer slept ī bedde fader syke sayd shulde neuer hole receyue sacramētys tyll sawe son sampson though ryght lothe goo yet counsell seynt iltute went vnto hym moche gladde cōmynge confessyd hym hym great hed synne longe kept close wyfe theyr chylderne betoke seruyce god sygne crosse kyllyd great serpent sayde celerer compleynyd wasted houy busshope dubryee thought proue sampson made sygne crosse ouer vessellys anon vessellys whiche hadde afore geuyn almes fyllyd agayne full hony abbot thre yerys wente scotlande dyd many great myracles instructyd people came whome dubrycyus commaundement aungell made hym busshope went lytyll brytayne foūde man seesyde lokynge oon shewyd hym lorde shulde come fro yonde see shuld hele wyfe lepoure doughter vexyd deuyll soo helyd theym bothe quene great malyce vnto hym gaue hym puyson turnyd wylde lyon hym escapyd worde lyon dyed quene seynge myracle askyd hym forgyuenes euery lent wolde secret place fro recourse people departyd fro lyfe fyth kalendas auguste lyeth monasterye dolo foundyd lytle brytayne doon dyuerse monasteryes blessyd man suche grace euer masse aungells assyste hym mynystre hym sacryfyce ¶de sanctum sexburga regina abbatissa seynt sexburghe doughter anna kynge eest englonde maryed ercombertus kynge kent hadde issue egbertus lotharyus whiche kyngys two doughters ermenylde erkēgode hyghe degre meke poore mekenes folowyd example suster deth made abbesse moche dylygent cause knewe cure charge endyd present lyfe daye nonas iulii aboute yere lorde vic xl buryed suster ¶de sancto swithuno ep̄o confessore ryche men poore men euer callyd vppon synners penaūce encouragyd men lyuyd vertuously perseuer vertue neuer toke full meale moderatly sustenaunce longe vygyllys great labourys shuld fayle toke lytyll hole agayne euer busy psalmes spirituell melodye dylygence kept herte clennes ꝑseuered kepynge cōmaudementes lorde departynge worlde whiche syxth nonas iulii yere lorde god dccclxii translated yere lorde dcccclxxi ide iulii daye translacyon lorde shewyd hym many myracles thilde contracte fro byrth helyd blynde wymmen syght yrons one pryson brake man delyuered man syke palsey helyd xxv also made hole dyuers sykenes ¶de sancto thatheo confessore seynt thathe sone kynge itlande called thathalius fro yonge age kepte hym self vndefowled fro al vyces fader moder sawe hym despyse worldy thynges set hym scole profyted moche vertue cōnynge countre yonge folkes came doctryne fader syke called haue taken charge realme aungell appered hym aduertysed hym kepe firste purpose nat coueyt desceytfull enheritaūce worlde sayd se shall shortly vanysshe away wt heuynes ꝑell ye mornynge viii felowes went wale shyp without sayle ore when̄e come ouer restynge theym towne therby sent one tye bote came ī ye messenger founde harte holdynge rope sauynge bote fro drownynge harte ledde seynt thathe ye power god lay downe ye groū de stretched hed made sygnes shuld kylled make mete bretherne desyre kynge called cradoke gathered many scolers made churche blessyd trinyte counseyll bysshop landaffe sette xii chanons kynges seruaūtes theyr horse destroyed grounde sodeynly horse dyed kynge herde came hym cryed hym mercy anone horse rose agayne kynge seynge ye myracle gaue hym ye towne owne palays seruauntes kynge gundlens stale cowe kylled seth cawdren seth rawer seynt thathe herynge therof folowed way founde prynt fote meruaylously prynted stone folowed kynges palays whereof malyce mockage euyll seruauntes couered cawdren made lyke sete syt downe theron shuld haue ben skalded hym satte downe harde sure kyng heryng therof kneled downe asked hym mercy made ye flesshe bone layde skynne cowe anone rose vp afore theym seynt cadoke sone kynge seyng myracle became disciple many vertuous werkes came hym whiche receyued mekely wassynge theyr handes fete sodeynly one theym gone nyght folowynge aungell appered one brethene sayd geste ye day byfore went sodeynly fro addyng therto yt appoynted northe partes put hym selfe seruyce man towne tauerham great gyuer almes moche gaue nat oonly owne mete poore men also tyme gaue shone poore man went hym selfe barefote whenne dame perceyued feyned hadde great nede haue thornes caused hym go wodde fet theym home goodnes oure lorde thornes hym lyke rose flower hurtynge hym thynge whenne dame knewe cryed hym mercy anone forgaue mayster seynge honestly came chambre ranne pryuely towarde churche ꝑceyued ī great angre folowed ouer taken hylle wolde wyse assent hym strake hedde hedde fell anone sprange fayre welle stone therof haue redde probacyon therfore nowe thowe arte prouyd procede make redy tyme come yt promysyd yt shalbe fulfyllyd yt saye yt myn aulter thou shalte clothyd cō secrate nunne hensforthe thou shalte onely reputyd ioye shall receyue wordys heuenly reuelacyons haue shemyd thynges haue sayde shalbe fulfyllyd though grace withdrawen fro many theyr vnkyndenes neuerthelesse shall come shall ryse theyr place whiche shall opteyne grace mornynge fyfte daye nowe nexte folowynge thou haste receyuyd sacramētys chyrche calle seuerallye persones haue namyd nowe telle theym shall doo theyr handy thou shalte come ioye euerlastynge thy bodye shall caryed watzstenes sayde fyfte daye callyd hyr hyr housholde shewyd theym shulde doo laste gaue great monycyon hyr son byrgerus hyr doughter katheryne chargynge theym aboue thynges shulde perseuer drede god loue theyr neyghbourys good warkys theropon made hyr confessyon great dylygens deuocyon receyuynge blessyd bodye oure lorde noylyd masse sayde afore hyr honouryd rome whiche fro hyr byrthe great grosse throte moche foule dyfformyd came bodye seynt byrgette hyr owne gyrdell towchyd ye hande gloryous woman seynt byrgette great deuocyon bounde ye gyrdell abowte birgette anon infaun •• beganne waxe hote take brethe afterwarde restoryd full lyfe wherfore moder great deuocyon gladnes fulfyllynge hyr auowe vysytyd relykes seynt birgette monasterye watzstenes aboute natyuyte oure lorde certeyne person gothlande toke see great tempeste dryuen place whiche moche shalowe water theyr shyppe broysyd taryed se nyght great hunger colde coulde remoue theyr shyppe wekys ende asmoche lyke haue perysshyd lacke sustenaū ce drewe cuttes amonge theym whiche theym shulde kyllyd made mete vppon whome lotte felle great wepynge commyttyd hym seynt birgette prayde helpe promysynge escapyd daunger wolde vysyte hyr hyr monasterye watzstenes anon myracle foūde great peace flesshe see hadde refresshyd theym selfe therwyth arose anon suche great calmenes lytell smalle bote came great longe weyes see londe vpon whome lotte felle goynge towarde watzstenes fulfyll vowe waye takyn prysoner greuously betyn leyde prysone many iron vpon hym wherfore estesones prayde seynt birgette helpe anon hadde doon iron bondys felle fro hym toke iourney towarde seynt birgette withoute lette great deuocion cytie lyptzyge peynter callyd hēry great loue hadde seynt birgette wonte sey many thynges amonge doctours hyr holynes bookys hyr heuenly reuelacyons wherfore tyme oon doctours great indygnacyon sayd vnto hym thou leuesayde speke thys newe • esye bokys olde matrone shall cause burnyd thy erroure porposyd haue causyd paynter cytyd daye folowynge shuld appere iuges wherupon sayde peynter wente clerke also great denocyon seynt birgette aske hym coūceyle comfortyd hym ryghte charytably aduysyd hym dylygent prayer almyghtye god seynt birgette bade hym drede nothynge wolde helpe hym ouer sayde another preest callyd master iohn̄ torto whiche also great deuocion seynt birgette wolde praye hym seynt birgette dydde mornynge sayde peynter beynge moch ferefull apperyd ye iuges strayghtly examynyd many thynges leyde charge haue conuyctyd hym heresye prayer seynt birgette sufferde trowble sayde symple laye man letterde fulfyllyd holy goste speke soo effectuouslye great hyghe mysteryes almyghtye god aduersaryes coulde resyste ye spyryt speke hym wherfore dyschargyd aduersaryes confysyd longe oure lorde toke vengeaunce hym pryncypall causer dysturbaunce went nyght hoole bedde nyght smytten fallynge sykenes wherof dyed anon bodye rottyd corruptyd suche horryble stenche fewe men durste come nyghe handelynge body flesche came bonys great peace laste men horryble sauoure refusyd bere hym graue certeyne ꝑsonys vsyd clensevyle stynkynge pryuyes hyryd bere wretchyd bodye graue whenne hadde sayde hadde knowen horryble sauoure wolde haue borne hym though myght haue dowble pryce hadde finis prayer seynt byrgette ¶nowe lette v pray vnto gloryous spouse sauyoure cryste ihesu seynt byrgette praye v vnto lorde merytys hyr prayer transytory short lyfe maye come euerlastynge lyfe blysse heuyn amen ¶a prayer seynt byrgette birgitta mater bona dulcis ductrix et patron • nobis fer suffragia naufragantes hoc mari tuo ductusalutari duc ad vite breuia preclara tu dignare delictorum impetrare nobis christi veniam ut possimus respirare et excessus emendare consecuti gratiam confer vite sanctitatem corpori da sanitatem et quieta tempora auge veram charitatem cordium da puritatem no languentes robora uite nostre rege cursum post hanc vitam transfersursum anima ad gaudia ubi deum contemplari tibi quo que sociari possimus gloria amen uersus ¶ora pro nobis beata birgitta sponsa christi preelecta ut ad celestem patriā sit ipse nobis via rectum oremꝰ deus qui ecclesiam tuā per beatam birgittam sacris illuminare dignatus e et cōsiliis exemplis cōcede propicius eius intercessionevt que pro nostris purgandis excessibus clementer ei reuelasti deuotis mentibus exequamur per christum • n̄m nostrum amen ¶another prayer seynt byrgette beata birgi • ta late collandata principissa suecie terris vocata uita verbo stabilis solide fundata omnibus affabilis humilis monstrata post sponsi exequias casta approbata remotas prouincias e peregrinata cristo sponsa nobilis pie adoptata nunc mane laudabilis christo copulata sanctorum reliquias pietate grata deuotis obsequiis multum venerata multis misteriis aliis prelata coruscas miraculis celo sublimata iustis desideriis assiste perata regnis et ecclesie pace confirmata pro nostris miseriis matrona beata sponsa sponsum dominum flecte aduocata uersus multe filie regum congregauerunt diuicias tu superegressa e vniuersas oratio domine ihesu criste qui beatam birgittā propter multorum secretorum inspiracionem et singularem virtutum adornacionem sponsam tuam vocari decreuisti presta quesumus vt eadem vite moribus conformemur cum ea de mundi illecebris ad visionem celestium transferamur qui viuis regnas c ¶thus endyth lyfe seynt byrgette enprynted lōdon flere strete sygne george rycharde pynson prynter vnto kynges noble grace xx daye february yere oure lorde god ccccc xvi hereaftre foloweth deuoute boke compylyd mayster walter hylton deuoute man temperall estate howe shulde rule hym whiche ryghte expedyent euery man moste especyall theym lyue medylde lyfe shewyth medelyd lyfe wyll dylygently loke vpon may therby soner come ye hyghe vertues blessyd lyfe shall rede begynnynge present boke gloryous seyntys conteynyd ¶howe man yt woll ghostly must fyrste vse moche bodely exercyse penaunce destroyenge synne capitulum primum dere broder ī cryst two maner state holy chyrche crystē soulys please god get theym blysse heuyn one bodely ghostly bodely werkynge longeth pryncypally worldly men wymen ye lefully vse worldlye goodes wylfully vse worldlye busynes also longeth yonge begynnynge men comen newe worldly synnys ye seruyce god make theym able ghostly werkynge breke downe yt vnbuxumnes body dyscrecyon suche bodelye werkynge myghte souple redy moche cōtraryous spyryte ghostly werkynge seynt poule sayth woman made man man woman ryght bodely werkynge made ghostly ghostly bodely bodely werkynge goth ghostly cōmyth seynt poule sayeth ¶non ꝙ prius spirituale sed ꝙ prius animale deinde spirituale cause behouyth ar borne synne corrupcyon flesshe ar blyndyd ouerlayed yt haue neyther ghostlye knowynge god lyght vnderstandynge ne ghostlye felynge hym clene desyre louynge therfore may sodeynly sterte derke nyght flesshly corrupcyon yt ghoostly lyghte may suffre ne bere syknes selfe may bodely eyen whan sore beholde ye lyght son therfore must abyde werke processe tyme fyrst bodyly werkys bysyly tyll dyschargyd heuy burden synne whiche lettyth v fro ghostlye werkynge tyll soules somwat clensyd fro great outwarde synnes abled ghostly werke bodyly werkynge yt speke mayste thou vnderstōde manner good werkys yt thy soule dothe ye wyttes mēbrys thy body vnto thy selfe fastynge wakyng restraynynge flesshely lustes penaūce doynge thyn euen crysten fullfyllynge ye dedys mercy bodely ghostly vnto god sufferynge bodely myscheuys ye loue ryghwysenes thy se werkys done trouth charyte please god without nought desyrythe occupyed ghostly syker profytable hym yt fyrste well assayde longe tyme bodely werkyng bodely dedys tokē shewynge morall vertues withoute whiche soule able werke ghostlye breke downe fyrste pryde bodely berynge also within thy harte thynkynge bostynge praysynge thy selfe vayn lykynge ī thy selfe ony thynge yt god hath sent ye bodely ghostly breke downe also enuy yre agaynste thyn euēcrysten whether ryche poore good bad thou hate hym ne haue dysdeyne hym wylfully neyther worde ne dede also breke downe couetyse worldly good thou holdynge gettynge sauynge offende thy concyence ne breke charyte god thyn euyncrysten loue ony worly good thou gettyst kepe spēde without loue vayne lykynke reason askyth worshyp god helpe thyn euencrysten breke downe also moch thou mayst flesshly lykynges eyther accydye bodely ease glotony lechery whan thou hast ben • l traueylyd well asayde suche bodely werkys mayste thou grace ordeyne ghostlye werkynge ¶howe man set ghostly lyuynge shall rule dedys dyscrecyon without turne often vyce ca ii grace goodnes lord ihesu cryst hathe shewyd withdrawynge thyn herte fro luste lykynge worldlye vanyte vse flesshely synnys turnynge thy wyll entyerly seruyce plesaunce bryngeth myn herte moche mater loue hym mercy also steryth greatlye strēgthe thy good purpose thy werkynge thou haste begonne brynge good ende coulde pryncypally god sythen tēder affeccyon loue yt thou haste wretche vnworthy knowe well desyre thyn herte yt thou desyrest greatlye serue lord ghostly occupacyon holly withouten lettynge troublynge worldlye busynes yt thou myghtest come grace knowyng ghostlye felynge god ghostly thynges desyre good hope god set vpon hym charyte spyrytually neuerthelesse refrayne rule dyscrescyon agaynste outwarde werkynge ye state thou arte charyte vnrulyd tourneth somtyme vyce therfore sayde holy wrytte ¶ordinauit charitatem saye lorde geuynge charyte set ordre rule shulde loste thrugh myn vndyscressyon ryght charyte desyre lorde hath geuyn mercy rule ordeyne thou shalt pursue thy degre askyth lyuynge thou hast vsyd tyme ye grace vertues thou haste thou shalt vtterly folowe thy desyre leue occupacyon busynes worldle ye ar nedefull vse rewlynge thy selfe vnder thy kepynge geue holly ghostly occupacyon prayer holy medytacyons frere monke man yt bounde worlde chyldren seruaūtys thou arte fallyth thou soo thou kepyst order charyte ¶also thou woldyst leue vtterly ghostly occupacyon namemely grace god hath geuyn set holly busynes worlde fulfyllynge werkes actyfe lyfe fully man neuer felyd deuocyon thou leuyst ordre charyte thy state askyth bothe eche dyuerse tymes thou shalte medle werkys actyfe lyfe ghostely werkys lyfe cōtemplatyfe doest thou well thou shalte one tyme busye martha rule gouerne thyn husholde thy chyldren thy seruauntys thy neyghbourys thy tenauntys doo well cōforte theym therin helpe doo euyll teche mende thē chastyse theym thou shalt also loke know wysely thy thynges thy worldly goodes ryghtfully kepte thy seruauntys gouernyd truely spendyd yt thou myght ye plēteuously fulfyll ye dedys mersy vnto thy euen crysten also thou shalt marye leue busynes worlde sytte downe foot lorde mekenes prayer holy thoughtys contemplacyon hym geuyth grace shalt thou goo fro one medefully fulfyll theym bothe kepeste thou well order charyte ¶unto maner mā belōgyth actyf lyfe ca iii neuerthelesse thou ne haue wonder yt say therfore shall tell declare lytyll openlye thou shalte vnderstande yt thre maners lyuynge one actyfe lyfe another contemplatyfe thyrde made bothe medelyd actyfe lyfe aboue longeth worldlye men wymen whych lewde knowyng ghostlye occupacyon ne fele sauour ne deuocion feruoure loue men doo ne canne skylle yet neuerthelesse haue drede god payne hell therfore flee synne haue desyre please god come heuyn good wyll haue ther euēcrysten vnto thyse men nedefull spedefull vse werkys actyflyfe busylye maye helpe themselfe theyr euencrysten canne elles doo ¶unto belongyth contemplatyfe lyfe ca iiii contemplatyfe lyfe longeth alone men wymen ye loue god forsake open synnes worlde theyr flesshe busynes charge gouernaunce worldly goodes make selfe poore nakyd bare nede bodyly kynde flee fro souereynte men seruyce god vnto thyse men longeth traueyle occupye inwardly gete thrughe grace lorde clennes herte pea concyens destroyinge synne receyuynge vertues soo come contemplacyon clennes may without great exarcyse body contynuell trauayle spirit deuout prayer feruent desyres ghostly medyracyons ¶unto belongeth medlyd lyfe ca v thyrde lyfe ye medlyd lyfe lōgeth men bodyly chyrche prelatys curatys whiche haue cure soueraynte ouer men teche rule thē bothe theyr bodyes theyr soulys pryncipally fulfyllynge dedys mercy bodelye ghostly vnto thyse men longyth somtyme vse werkys mercy actyfe lyfe helpe sustenaunce selfe theyr subgiettys also sōtyme leue maner busynes outwarde gyue theym vnto prayer medytacyons redynge holy wryt ghostly occupacyōs yt fele disposyd also lōgeth tēporall men haue souereynte moch fauer worldlye goodes haue also lordshyp ouer men gouerne susteyne fader hath ouer chyldren mayster ouer seruaūtis lorde ouer tenaūtys ye whiche men haue also receyuyd lordes gyfte grace deuocyon ī party sauoure ghostly occupacyon unto men also lōgeth medlyd lyfe yt actyfe contemplatyfe thyse men stōdynge ye charge ye bōde yt haue takyn wyll leue vtterly yt busynes worde ought skylfully vsyd ī fulfyllynge charge holly gyue cōtēplatyf lyfe well kepe ye ordre charyte charyte thou knowyst well lyeth bothe loue god thyn euencristen therfore yt yt hath charyte vse bothe werkynke yt one nowe yt yt ye loue god cōtemplacyon leuyth loue euencristen doth ought whan boūde therto fulfyllyth charyte also ye contraye wyse hath great regarde werke actyfe lyfe busynes ye worlde yt loue euēcristen leuyth gostly occupacyō vtterly yt god hath dysposyd hym therto fulfyllyth charyte sayinge seynt gregory though lorde styre vse medlyd lyfe toke vpon hym selfe persone maner men prelatis holy chyrch suche disposed therto haue sayd gaue ensaumple owne werkynge yt shuld vse medlyd lyfe dyd one tyme cōmonyd wt men medlyd wt wynge dedys mercy theym taught vncōnynge vnknowen prechynge vysityd syke helyd theym theyr dyseasys fed ye hūgry cōfortyd yt sory neuerthelesse tymes lefte ye cōuersacyō worldly men dyscyples went desert vpon ye hyllys cōtynued nyght prayer alone gospell sayth therfore medlyd lyfe wyth lord hym selfe ensaūple men yt haue takyn charge medlyd lyfe yt shuld one tyme gyue thē busynes worldly thyngys resonable nede werkys actyfe lyfe profyt theyr euencrysten whiche haue cure tyme gyue holly deuocyon contemplacyon prayer medytacyons ¶how holy busshops vsyd medlyd lyfe ca vi lyfe ledde holy busshopys cure mennys soules mynystracyon temporall goodes thyse holy men lefte vtterly mynystracyon lokynge dyspendynge worldly goodes gaue holly cōtemplacyon moch grace contemplacyon hadde lefte full ofte theyr owne rest contemplacyon whan yt well leuer haue byn stylle loue theyr euyncrystē entermetyd worldly busynes ī helpynge ther subgyettys southly charyte wysely dyscretly departyd theyr lyuynge two tyme fulfyllyd lower parte charyte werkys actyfe lyfe bounde therto takynge prelacye tyme fullfyllyd hygher partye charyte contemplacyon god ghostly thynges prayer medytacyons charyte god ther euencrysten affeccyon soule within also shewynge bodyly dedys without men yt oonly contemplatyfe fre fro curys prelacye full charyte god theyr euencrysten oonly affeccyon theyr soule outwarde shewynge hap soo moche full inwarde yt myght ne nedyd ne fyll shewe outwarde theyse men prelacye also yt onely temporall men full charyte affeccyon within also werkynge properly medlyd lyfe bothe actyfe cō templatyfe lyfe southly suche man inspyrytuell souereynte prelatis curatys temporall souereynte worldly lordes maysters holde medlyd lyfe best moost behouefull longe bounden therto free bounde temporall mynystracyon ne spyrytuall hope lyfe contemplatyfe alone myght come therto southfastly best moost spedefull moost medefull moost fayre moost worthy vse holde leue wylfully outwarde warkynge actyfe lyfe great nede great releuynge comfortynge men eyther theyr bodyes theyr soules nede aske ye prayer instaūce ellys byddynge souerayne hope good shewe thē outwarde werkys actyf lyfe tyme helpynge theyr euecrysten ¶what lyfe moost accordyd hym wrytten man hath souerentye shall gyue hym vtterly deuociō leue wordly busynes ca vii haue sayde partye mayste thou vnderstonde whiche oon whiche accordyth moost thy state lyuynge southly methynkyth medlyd lyfe accordyth moost sythen lorde hath ordeynyd set state soueraynte ouer men moche hath lent abūdaūce worldly goodes rule susteyne specyally thyse yt vnder thy gouernaūce thy lordshyp thy myghte connynge also therwith thou haste receyuyd grace ye mercy lorde knowe thy selfe gostly desyre sauoure loue hope yt thys lyfe yt medlyd beste accordyth ye trauayle therfore deꝑte wysely thy lyuynge wyt thou well thou leue nedefull busynes actyfe lyfe rekles take kepe thy worldly goodes arspēdyd kepte ne makyst force thy subiectys thy euencrysten cause desyre wyll yt thou hast geue ye ghostly occupacyō wenynge yt thou arte yt excused thou thou doest wysly ar thy werkys worth whether bodyly ghostly done rightfully resonably ye worshyp god byddynge southly ryght noughte thou leue yt thynge yt thou arte boūde ye way charyte ryght reson wylt holly gyue ye thinge wylfully plesaunce god whiche thou art fully boūde thou doest worshype dyscretly hym thou arte busy worshyp hed face araye fayre curyously thou leuest body yt foot raggyd rent takest kepe therof thou worshypest hym vylany worshyp mā curyouslye arayed vpō hed perlys precyous stonys body nakyd bare begger ryght ghostly worshyp god crowne hed leue body bare thou shalt vndertonde yt lord ihesu cryste man hed ghostly bodye holy chyrche ye mēbres body crystenyd men armes foot mēbres sūdry werkynges yt vse theyr lyuynge thā yt thou busy wt thy myghte aray hed yt worshype hym selfe mynde passyon werkys manhed deuocyō medytacyō hym forgettyst foot yt ar thy chyldren thy seruaūtys thy tenaūtys thyn euēcrysten letyst thē spyll defaute kepynge vnarayed vnkept tent ought thou pleasyst hym thou est worshyp hym thou makest yt kysse mothe deuocyon ghostly prayer thou tredest vpon foot defoulyst moche thou wylt tende neclygēce thy selfe ye thou haste take cure thus thynkyth neuertheles thou thynke yt south feyre offyce worshyp hed hym daye occupyed medytacion ye manhed go lower werkys make clene foot busy bothe worde ī dede aboute ye helpe thyn euēcrysten thynke southly wyll thanke meke wasshynge foot whan right foule stynke vpō ye precyous peyntynge arayenge yt thou canst make aboute hedde mynde manhed fayre inoughe nedythe arayed ye moch fet mēbrys yt somtyme euyll arayed nede lokyd holpen namely sythen thou arte boūde therto therfore wyll cūne thanke yf thou wylt mekely tēderly loke thē ye lower seruyce yt thou doest thy lorde ye loue hym mēbres whan nede ryght askyth wt glad meke herte ye pleasyst thou hym thynkynge yt ynough ye leest degre lowyst state sythen wyll yt semyth sythen hath put ye yt state traueyle serue men well done thou shuldest fulfyll thy myght ensaumple saye ye thou doest thus saye hope yt thou doest thus better wolde thou shuldest doo thus gladly thynke loth leue somtyme ghostly occupacyon entermete worldly busynes wyse kepyng spendynge thy worldly goodes good rulynge thy seruaū • y thy tenaūtys good werkys werkynge thyn euyncrysten thy myght thou shuldest doo bothe werkys dyuers tymes good wyll one thou myghtyst thou haddest prayed ben occupyed ghostly thou shalt certeyne tyme breke shalte thou busyly gladlye occupye bodyly occupacyon thyn euen crysten also whanne thou haste ben busye outwarde whyle thy seruauntys men profytably thou shalte breke turne agayne thy prayer thy deuocyons god geuyth grace shalt thou
